25:T274c,<entryFree id="n41692" key="وَجَدَهُ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">وَجَدَهُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِدُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">يَجُدُ</foreign>, (S, L, Msb, K,) the latter of the dial. of the tribe of 'Ámir (S, L, Msb) Ibn-Saasa'ah, (MF,) and without a parallel (S, L, Msb, K) in verbs of this class, (S, L, Msb,) the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> in it being dropped because it falls out in the original form of the aor., (Msb,) both of which forms are said by several authors to apply to the verb in all its significations, though F seems to restrict the latter to two significations, (TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">وُجُودٌ</foreign> (S, L, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">وِجْدَان</foreign> (L, Msb, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">إِجْدَانٌ</foreign>, (IAar, L, K,) in which the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> is changed into <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>, (L,) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">وُجْدٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جِدَةٌ</foreign>; (L, K;) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجِدَهُ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِدُ</foreign>; (K;) but this form of the verb is not found in the lexicons, [the K only accepted,] (MF,) in the sense here assigned to it; (TA;) <hi rend="ital">He found it; lighted on it; attained it; obtained it by searching</hi> or <hi rend="ital">seeking; discovered it; perceived it; saw it; experienced it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became sensible of it;</hi> (F, in the K and in the Basáïr, on the authority of Abu-l-Kásim El-Isbahánee;) namely, a thing sought, sought for or after, or desired; (S, L, K;) and simply a thing. (L.) <foreign lang="ar">وُجُود</foreign> is of several kinds. It is The <hi rend="ital">finding, &amp;c., by means of any one of the five senses:</hi> as when one says <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدْتُ زَيْدًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I found, &amp;c., Zeyd</hi>]: and <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَتُ طَعْمَهُ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">رَائِحَتَهُ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">صَوْتَهُ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">خُشُونَتَهُ</foreign>, [<hi rend="ital">I found,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">perceived, &amp;c., its taste,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">its odour,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">its sound,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">its roughness</hi>]. Also, The <hi rend="ital">finding, &amp;c., by means of the faculty of appetite,</hi> [<hi rend="ital">or rather of sensation,</hi> which is the cause of appetite:] as when one says <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الشِّبَعَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I found, experienced,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became sensible of, satiety</hi>]. Also, The <hi rend="ital">finding, &amp;c., by the intellect,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">by means of the intellect:</hi> of which kind is one's knowing God: and here it should be observed, that <foreign lang="ar">وجود</foreign> attributed to God is simple knowledge: (Abu-l-Kásim El-Isbahánee, cited in the Basáïr:) <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ ٱللّٰهُ</foreign>, wherever it occurs, means <hi rend="ital">God knew.</hi> (Er-Rághib, Z, &amp;c.) i. e., in the Kur-án. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He found, in the sense of</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he knew</hi> [<hi rend="ital">by experience</hi>]. (A, TA, &amp;c.) [In this sense, it is a verb of the kind called <foreign lang="ar">أَفْعَالُ القُلُوبِ</foreign>; having two objective complements; the first of which is called its noun, and the second its predicate.] Ex. <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">زَيْدًا ذَا الحِفَاظِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I</hi> [<hi rend="ital">found,</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">knew Zeyd to possess the quality of defending those things which should be sacred,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">inviolable.</hi> (A.) Used in this sense, as doubly trans., its inf. n. is <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدَانٌ</foreign> (Akh) and <foreign lang="ar">وُجُودٌ</foreign>. (Seer.) It is also used as singly trans., as syn. with <foreign lang="ar">عَلِمَ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  When <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he found,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">lighted on,</hi> a thing after it had gone away, its inf. n. is <foreign lang="ar">وِجْدَانٌ</foreign>. (IKtt.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ الضَّالَّةَ</foreign>, (S, A, Msb,) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِد</foreign> (Msb) and <foreign lang="ar">يَجُدُ</foreign>, (MF,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدَانٌ</foreign> (S, Msb) and <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ أَجِدْ مِنْ ذٰلِكَ بُدًّا</foreign> (Msb) [<hi rend="ital">He found the stray beast</hi>].          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ أَجِدْ مِنْ ذٰلِكَ بُدًّا</foreign>, for which one also says <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ اجدِ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">I found no means of avoiding,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">escaping, that.</hi> (Kz, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ</foreign>, (L,) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ فِى المَالِ</foreign>, (Fs, T, S, L, Msb,) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ المَالَ وَغَيَرَهُ</foreign>, (Lh, M, K,) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِدُ</foreign>, (Lh, M, L, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">وُجْد</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">وِجد</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جِدَهٌ</foreign> (Lh, T, S, M, K) and <foreign lang="ar">وِجْدَانٌ</foreign> (T, L) and <foreign lang="ar">وُجُودٌ</foreign>, (Yz,) <hi rend="ital">He became possessed of wealth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">property:</hi> (T:) or <hi rend="ital">he was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, rich; possessed of competence,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sufficiency; in no need; without wants,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">with few wants;</hi> (S, M, L, K;) <hi rend="ital">so as not to be poor afterwards:</hi> (L:) and <hi rend="ital">he gained, acquired,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">earned wealth.</hi> (Exps. of the Fs.) Hence the saying of the Arabs, <foreign lang="ar">وِجْدَانُ الرَّقِينِ يُغَطِّى أَفَنَ الأَفِينِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The possession of money hides the weakness of judgment of the weak in judgment</hi>]. (T, L.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign>, (S, L, K, &amp;c.) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِدُ</foreign> (Fs, M, L, K) and <foreign lang="ar">يَجُدُ</foreign>; (M, L, K;) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجِدَ</foreign>, as heard by Fr from certain of the Arabs; (Kzz;) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">مَوْجِدَةٌ</foreign>, (Fs, S, A, L, Msb, K,) by some pronounced <foreign lang="ar">مَوْجَدَةٌ</foreign>, (Fr,) and <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جِدَةٌ</foreign> (L, K) and <foreign lang="ar">وِجْدَانٌ</foreign> (Lh, S, M, L) and <foreign lang="ar">وُجُودٌ</foreign> (Fr, Kzz) <hi rend="ital">He was angry with him:</hi> (Fs, S, A, L, Msb, K) or <hi rend="ital">he was angry with him with the anger that proceeds from a friend.</hi> (TA, voce <foreign lang="ar">عَتْبٌ</foreign>.)       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ بِهِ</foreign>, (aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجِدُ</foreign>, L,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">وَجْدٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">He loved him.</hi> (L, K.) <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ بِهَا</foreign>, (A, L,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n41692-1" target="توّجد" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (A,) <hi rend="ital">He loved her;</hi> (A, L;) <hi rend="ital">he loved her passionately</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fondly.</hi> (L.) <foreign lang="ar">لَهُ بِهَا وَجْدٌ</foreign>
